Custom likelihood function¶

Note that to run the custom log-likelihood function you need to specify which X variables correspond to which event (this is done in _ll_ols) near ####.

Also it is wise to specify initialization values for the parameters. This can be done in MyOLS by ####.

In [5]:
def _ll_ols(y, X, params):

    ####
    
    # Create X matrix and parameters with only default variables
    X_def = X[:,0:6]
    params_def = params[0:6]
    
    # Create X matrix and parameters with only prepay variables
    X_pre = X[:,6:12]
    params_pre = params[6:12]
    
    e_X_def_beta = np.exp(np.matmul(X_def,params_def))
    e_X_pre_beta = np.exp(np.matmul(X_pre,params_pre))
    denom = 1 + e_X_def_beta + e_X_pre_beta
    
    def_log_probabilities = np.log(e_X_def_beta/denom)           
    pre_log_probabilities = np.log(e_X_pre_beta/denom)
    
    nothing_log_probabilities = np.log(1/denom)        
                                         
    log_liklihood = 0
    log_liklihood = np.matmul(def_log_probabilities,y[:,0])
    log_liklihood += np.matmul(pre_log_probabilities,y[:,1])
    log_liklihood += np.matmul(nothing_log_probabilities,y[:,2])                                     
    
    print(params)
    print(log_liklihood)
    
    return (log_liklihood)
In [6]:
class MyOLS(GenericLikelihoodModel):
    def __init__(self, endog, exog, **kwds):
        super(MyOLS, self).__init__(endog, exog, **kwds)
    
    def nloglikeobs(self, params):
        ll = _ll_ols(self.endog, self.exog, params)
        return -ll
    
    def fit(self, start_params=None, maxiter=50000, maxfun=5000, **kwds):

        if start_params == None:
            # Reasonable starting values
            
            ####
            start_params = (np.random.rand(self.exog.shape[1])-.5)
            
            start_params[0] = -6
            start_params[1] = 0
            start_params[2] = 0
            start_params[3] = 0
            
            start_params[6] = -4
            start_params[7] = 0
            start_params[8] = 0
            start_params[9] = 0
            
            print(self.exog.shape)
        return super(MyOLS, self).fit(start_params=start_params,
                                      maxiter=maxiter, maxfun=maxfun,**kwds)

Import data and fit a small model¶

In [7]:
data_all = pd.read_hdf('sample_data_factors.h5',start=0,stop=100000)

# drop credit score NA
data_all = data_all.dropna(subset=['credit score'])
data_all = data_all[data_all['credit score']<9999]
In [28]:
%%capture 
# To get rid of annoying warning

y = data_all[['default','prepay']]
y['nothing'] = 1-y['default']-y['prepay']

X = data_all[['age','Unemployment Rate','Real GDP YoY',
              'Treasury 30yr','Treasury 30yr_orig','credit score']]

# Transformed Variables
X['age_squared'] = X['age']**2
X['age_cubed'] = X['age']**3
X['30yr_diff'] = X['Treasury 30yr'] - X['Treasury 30yr_orig']

X['constant_def'] = 1
X['constant_pre'] = 1

# Specify ordering of X matrix
X = X[['constant_def','age','age_squared','age_cubed','credit score','Unemployment Rate',
       'constant_pre','age','age_squared','age_cubed','Real GDP YoY', '30yr_diff']]

X

In [30]:
X_def = X[['constant_def','age','age_squared','age_cubed','credit score','Unemployment Rate']]
X_pre = X[['constant_pre','age','age_squared','age_cubed','Real GDP YoY', '30yr_diff']]

# remove duplicated columns
X_def = X_def.loc[:,~X_def.columns.duplicated()]
X_pre = X_pre.loc[:,~X_pre.columns.duplicated()]

param_def = sm_ols_manual.params[0:6]
param_pre = sm_ols_manual.params[6:12]

X['prob_def'] = np.exp(np.matmul(X_def,param_def))/(1+np.exp(np.matmul(X_def,param_def))+np.exp(np.matmul(X_pre,param_pre)))
X['prob_pre'] = np.exp(np.matmul(X_pre,param_pre))/(1+np.exp(np.matmul(X_def,param_def))+np.exp(np.matmul(X_pre,param_pre)))
X['prob_other'] = 1 - X['prob_def'] - X['prob_pre']

X = X[['prob_def','prob_pre','prob_other']]

X

In [31]:
assess = data_all[['period','prepay','default','upb_prev']]
assess = X.merge(assess,left_index=True,right_index=True)

# put in expected prepay/default
assess['expected_prepay'] = assess['prob_pre']*assess['upb_prev']
assess['expected_default'] = assess['prob_def']*assess['upb_prev']

assess['actual_prepay'] = assess['prepay']*assess['upb_prev']
assess['actual_default'] = assess['default']*assess['upb_prev']

assess

In [32]:
grouped = assess
grouped['period'] = pd.DatetimeIndex(grouped['period']).year
grouped = assess.groupby('period')

# cum actual prepays/defaults
prepays = grouped['actual_prepay'].agg([np.sum])
defaults = grouped['actual_default'].agg([np.sum])

# cum expected prepays/defaults
e_prepays = grouped['expected_prepay'].agg([np.sum])
e_defaults = grouped['expected_default'].agg([np.sum])

plt.bar(x=prepays.index,height=prepays['sum'])
plt.bar(x=e_prepays.index,height=e_prepays['sum'],alpha=.5)
plt.title('Actual v Expected Prepays')
plt.show()
plt.bar(x=defaults.index,height=defaults['sum'])
plt.bar(x=e_defaults.index,height=e_defaults['sum'],alpha=.5)
plt.title('Actual v Expected Defaults')
plt.show()
